## 🔍 Cross-Page Patterns: Common HTML Issues

These HTML patterns cause the same accessibility errors across multiple pages. **Fix the pattern once in your codebase to fix it everywhere!**

### 🎯 Top Patterns to Fix (Highest Impact)

#### Pattern 1: Affects 100 page(s) - 200 occurrence(s)

**Scanner**: ALFA
**Rule**: [SIA-R73: Text spacing can be adjusted without loss of content](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r73)
**Issue**: The line height of the paragraph is less than 1.5

**HTML Pattern**:
```html
<p>...</p>
```

**XPath** (use in browser DevTools):
```
/p
```

**How to Replicate**:
1. Open any affected page in your browser
2. Press F12 to open DevTools
3. Go to Console tab
4. Run: `$x('/p')`
5. The element will be highlighted

**Affected Pages**:
- https://princeedwardisland.ca/
- https://princeedwardisland.ca/en/topic/find-health-services
- https://princeedwardisland.ca/en/topic/supports-and-services-5
- https://princeedwardisland.ca/en/information/emergency-medical-services-board
- https://princeedwardisland.ca/en/publication/alberton-public-library-report-to-the-community
- *...and 95 more page(s)*

---

#### Pattern 2: Affects 100 page(s) - 200 occurrence(s)

**Scanner**: ALFA
**Rule**: [SIA-R84: No description](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r84)
**Issue**: The scrollable element is not reachable through keyboard navigation

**HTML Pattern**:
```html
<div class="footer">...</div>
```

**XPath** (use in browser DevTools):
```
/div[@class="footer"]
```

**How to Replicate**:
1. Open any affected page in your browser
2. Press F12 to open DevTools
3. Go to Console tab
4. Run: `$x('/div[@class="footer"]')`
5. The element will be highlighted

**Affected Pages**:
- https://princeedwardisland.ca/
- https://princeedwardisland.ca/en/topic/find-health-services
- https://princeedwardisland.ca/en/topic/supports-and-services-5

**Rule**: [color-contrast](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/color-contrast?application=playwright)
**Impact**: serious
**Issue**: Elements must meet minimum color contrast ratio thresholds

**HTML Pattern**:

```
.btn
```

#### Pattern 6: Affects 100 page(s) - 100 occurrence(s)

**Scanner**: axe
**Rule**: [color-contrast](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/color-contrast?application=playwright)
**Impact**: serious
**Issue**: Elements must meet minimum color contrast ratio thresholds

**HTML Pattern**:
```html
<b>172.215.209.102</b>
```

**XPath** (use in browser DevTools):
```
b:nth-child(2)
```

**Scanner**: axe
**Rule**: [region](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/region?application=playwright)

**Issue**: All page content should be contained by landmarks

4. Run: `$x('body > .footer')`

#### Pattern 11: Affects 8 page(s) - 8 occurrence(s)

**Scanner**: axe
**Rule**: [scrollable-region-focusable](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/scrollable-region-focusable?application=playwright)
**Impact**: serious
**Issue**: Scrollable region must have keyboard access

**HTML Pattern**:
```html
<div class="footer">
```

**XPath** (use in browser DevTools):
```
.footer > .footer
```

4. Run: `$x('.footer > .footer')`

## Detailed Failure Information (ALFA)

### https://princeedwardisland.ca/

#### Rule: [SIA-R66: Text has enhanced contrast with its background](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r66)
**WCAG**: [SC 1.4.6](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/contrast-enhanced) (Level AAA)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The highest possible contrast of the text is 3.62:1 which is         below the required contrast of 7:1

#### Rule: [SIA-R69: Text has sufficient contrast with its background](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r69)
**WCAG**: [SC 1.4.3](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/contrast-minimum) (Level AA)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The highest possible contrast of the text is 3.62:1 which is         below the required contrast of 4.5:1

#### Rule: [SIA-R70](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r70)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The document contains deprecated elements

#### Rule: [SIA-R73: Text spacing can be adjusted without loss of content](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r73)
**WCAG**: [SC 1.4.12](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/text-spacing) (Level AA)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The line height of the paragraph is less than 1.5
- HTML: `<p>...but your activity and behavior on this site mad...</p>`
- XPath: `/p`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: The line height of the paragraph is less than 1.5
- HTML: `<p class="text-muted credit">...</p>`
- XPath: `/p[@class="text-muted credit"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R84](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r84)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The scrollable element is not reachable through keyboard navigation
- HTML: `<div class="footer">...</div>`
- XPath: `/div[@class="footer"]`

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The first tabbable element in the document is not a semantic link

- Message: The scrollable element is not reachable through keyboard navigation
- HTML: `<div class="footer">...</div>`
- XPath: `/div[@class="footer"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R87: First focusable element is a skip link](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r87)
**WCAG**: [SC 2.4.1](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/bypass-blocks) (Level A)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The first tabbable element in the document is not a semantic link

**WCAG**: [SC 1.4.12](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/text-spacing) (Level AA)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The line height of the paragraph is less than 1.5
- HTML: `<p>...but your activity and behavior on this site mad...</p>`
- XPath: `/p`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: The line height of the paragraph is less than 1.5
- HTML: `<p class="text-muted credit">...</p>`
- XPath: `/p[@class="text-muted credit"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R84](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r84)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The scrollable element is not reachable through keyboard navigation
- HTML: `<div class="footer">...</div>`
- XPath: `/div[@class="footer"]`

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The first tabbable element in the document is not a semantic link

**WCAG**: [SC 1.4.3](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/contrast-minimum) (Level AA)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The highest possible contrast of the text is 3.62:1 which is         below the required contrast of 4.5:1

#### Rule: [SIA-R70](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r70)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The document contains deprecated elements

#### Rule: [SIA-R73: Text spacing can be adjusted without loss of content](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r73)
**WCAG**: [SC 1.4.12](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/text-spacing) (Level AA)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The line height of the paragraph is less than 1.5
- HTML: `<p>...but your activity and behavior on this site mad...</p>`
- XPath: `/p`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: The line height of the paragraph is less than 1.5
- HTML: `<p class="text-muted credit">...</p>`
- XPath: `/p[@class="text-muted credit"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R84](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r84)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The scrollable element is not reachable through keyboard navigation
- HTML: `<div class="footer">...</div>`
- XPath: `/div[@class="footer"]`

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The first tabbable element in the document is not a semantic link

- XPath: `/p[@class="text-muted credit"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R84](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r84)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The scrollable element is not reachable through keyboard navigation
- HTML: `<div class="footer">...</div>`
- XPath: `/div[@class="footer"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R87: First focusable element is a skip link](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r87)
**WCAG**: [SC 2.4.1](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/bypass-blocks) (Level A)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The first tabbable element in the document is not a semantic link

#### Rule: [SIA-R73: Text spacing can be adjusted without loss of content](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r73)
**WCAG**: [SC 1.4.12](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/text-spacing) (Level AA)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The line height of the paragraph is less than 1.5
- HTML: `<p>...but your activity and behavior on this site mad...</p>`
- XPath: `/p`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: The line height of the paragraph is less than 1.5

## Detailed Failure Information (axe)

### https://princeedwardisland.ca/

#### Rule: [color-contrast](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/color-contrast?application=playwright)
**Impact**: serious
**WCAG**: [SC 1.4.3](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/contrast-minimum) (Level AA)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Elements must meet minimum color contrast ratio thresholds
- HTML: `<input type="submit" class="btn btn-success btn-sm" value="Submit">`
- XPath: `.btn`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: Elements must meet minimum color contrast ratio thresholds
- HTML: `<p class="text-muted credit"> 		You reached this page when trying to access 		<b>https://www.princeedwardisland.ca/</b> from 		<b>172.215.209.102</b> on 		<b>March 13 2026, 17:53:46 UTC</b> 	</p>`
- XPath: `.text-muted`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: Elements must meet minimum color contrast ratio thresholds
- HTML: `<b>https://www.princeedwardisland.ca/</b>`
- XPath: `.text-muted > b:nth-child(1)`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: Elements must meet minimum color contrast ratio thresholds
- HTML: `<b>172.215.209.102</b>`
- XPath: `b:nth-child(2)`

**Failure 5:**
- Message: Elements must meet minimum color contrast ratio thresholds
- HTML: `<b>March 13 2026, 17:53:46 UTC</b>`
- XPath: `b:nth-child(3)`

#### Rule: [landmark-one-main](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/landmark-one-main?application=playwright)
**Impact**: moderate

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Document should have one main landmark
- HTML: `<html lang="en">`
- XPath: `html`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: Document should have one main landmark
- HTML: `<html lang="en" data-id="hcaptcha-frame-5ea3feff9cf1292d7051510930d98c4719f64575">`
- XPath: `iframe[data-hcaptcha-widget-id="071hjp3rqrva"]`

#### Rule: [region](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/region?application=playwright)
**Impact**: moderate

**Failure 1:**
- Message: All page content should be contained by landmarks
- HTML: `<div class="container">`
- XPath: `.container`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: All page content should be contained by landmarks
- HTML: `<div class="footer">     <div class="footer"> 	<p class="text-muted credit"> 		You reached this page when trying to access 		<b>https://www.princeedwardisland.ca/</b> from 		<b>172.215.209.102</b> on 		<b>March 13 2026, 17:53:46 UTC</b> 	</p> </div> </div>`
- XPath: `body > .footer`

- HTML: `<div class="container">`
- XPath: `.container`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: All page content should be contained by landmarks
- HTML: `<div class="footer">`
- XPath: `body > .footer`

**Failure 1:**

- HTML: `<div class="footer"> 	<p class="text-muted credit"> 		You reached this page when trying to access 		<b>https://www.princeedwardisland.ca/en/information/innovation-pei/human-resources-planning-assistance</b> from 		<b>172.215.209.102</b> on 		<b>March 13 2026, 17:58:33 UTC</b> 	</p> </div>`

**WCAG**: [SC 1.4.3](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/contrast-minimum) (Level AA)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Elements must meet minimum color contrast ratio thresholds
- HTML: `<input type="submit" class="btn btn-success btn-sm" value="Submit">`
- XPath: `.btn`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: Elements must meet minimum color contrast ratio thresholds
- HTML: `<p class="text-muted credit"> 		You reached this page when trying to access 		<b>https://www.princeedwardisland.ca/en/publication/pdf-publication-carson</b> from 		<b>172.215.209.102</b> on 		<b>March 13 2026, 18:06:45 UTC</b> 	</p>`
- XPath: `.text-muted`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: Elements must meet minimum color contrast ratio thresholds
- HTML: `<b>https://www.princeedwardisland.ca/en/publication/pdf-publication-carson</b>`
- XPath: `.text-muted > b:nth-child(1)`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: Elements must meet minimum color contrast ratio thresholds
- HTML: `<b>172.215.209.102</b>`
- XPath: `b:nth-child(2)`

**Failure 5:**
- Message: Elements must meet minimum color contrast ratio thresholds
- HTML: `<b>March 13 2026, 18:06:45 UTC</b>`
- XPath: `b:nth-child(3)`

#### Rule: [landmark-one-main](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/landmark-one-main?application=playwright)
**Impact**: moderate

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Document should have one main landmark
- HTML: `<html lang="en">`
- XPath: `html`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: Document should have one main landmark
- HTML: `<html lang="en" data-id="hcaptcha-frame-5ea3feff9cf1292d7051510930d98c4719f64575">`
- XPath: `iframe[data-hcaptcha-widget-id="0p6gcfowzcv"]`

#### Rule: [region](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/region?application=playwright)
**Impact**: moderate

**Failure 1:**
- Message: All page content should be contained by landmarks
- HTML: `<div class="container">`
- XPath: `.container`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: All page content should be contained by landmarks
- HTML: `<div class="footer">     <div class="footer"> 	<p class="text-muted credit"> 		You reached this page when trying to access 		<b>https://www.princeedwardisland.ca/en/publication/pdf-publication-carson</b> from 		<b>172.215.209.102</b> on 		<b>March 13 2026, 18:06:45 UTC</b> 	</p> </div> </div>`

- HTML: `<div class="footer">     <div class="footer"> 	<p class="text-muted credit"> 		You reached this page when trying to access 		<b>https://www.princeedwardisland.ca/en/topic/gov-sub-topic-1</b> from 		<b>172.215.209.102</b> on 		<b>March 13 2026, 18:14:19 UTC</b> 	</p> </div> </div>`
- XPath: `body > .footer`

### https://princeedwardisland.ca/en/news/news-dec-11

**Impact**: serious
**WCAG**: [SC 1.4.3](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/contrast-minimum) (Level AA)
